<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">senat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">senātus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">council of <a href = vnd.unilang:elders.html>elders</a>; a senate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">senex</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">old</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***sepsis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sepsis.html>sepsis</a> (88258)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σῆψις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sêpsis</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">putrefaction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σήπειν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sḗpein</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make <a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σήψ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sḗps</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of lizard; also a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of serpent whose bite <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> alleged to cause putrefaction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sepsis.html>sepsis</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sepses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A serious medical condition in which the whole body <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> inflamed, causing injury to its own <a href = vnd.unilang:tissues.html>tissues</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:organs.html>organs</a> as a response to infection.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">antiseptic</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">asepsis</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">aseptic</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">septic</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:septicemia.html>septicemia</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">septicity</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:sepsis.html>sepsis</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:medisch.html>medisch</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ernstige.html>ernstige</a> ontstekingsreactie <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lichaam.html>lichaam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reactie.html>reactie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:infectie.html>infectie</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meestal.html>meestal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veroorzaakt.html>veroorzaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bacterie.html>bacteriën</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:producten.html>producten</a> (toxinen)</li></ol>

***septicemia.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:septicemia.html>septicemia</a> (99941)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span></span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sēpticus</i> + <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-emia</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:septicemia.html>septicemia</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">septicemias</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A disease caused by the presence of pathogenic organisms, especially bacteria, or their toxins, in the bloodstream, characterised by chills and fever.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">blood poisoning</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">septic fever</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">septicemic</span></li></ul>
</body>

***seraph.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:seraph.html>seraph</a> (63052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation of singular form plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">seraphim</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">seraphim</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">שרפים</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">serafim</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, plural form of <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">שרף</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">saraf</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The plural "seraphims" occurs in the King James Bible (Isaiah chapter 6).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the Oxford English Dictionary, the singular "<a href = vnd.unilang:seraph.html>seraph</a>" may have originated with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="w:John Milton">John Milton</a> who used it in Book I of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paradise_Lost" class="extiw" title="w:Paradise Lost">Paradise <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a></a> (1667).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:seraph.html>seraph</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">seraphs</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">seraphim</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">seraphims</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biblical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A six-winged angel; the highest choir or order of angels in Christian angelology, ranked above cherubim, and below <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>. They are the 5th highest order of angels in Jewish angelology. A detailed description can be found at the beginning of <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Bible_%28World_English%29/IsaiahChapter_6">Isaiah chapter 6</a></li></ol>
</body> 
***sere.html

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sēro</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sêer</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-e</i>.

<ol><li>strongly, very, to a great degree</li>
<li>hard, forcefully</li>
<li>fast, with speed</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sēsamum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σήσαμον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sḗsamon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Old <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aramaic" class="extiw" title="w:Aramaic">Aramaic</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="arc">שושמא</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šūššmā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, shortening of <i class="Hebr mention" lang="arc">שומשומא</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šumššemā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akkadian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Akkadian language">Akkadian</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="akk">𒃻𒈦𒌑𒈬</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ts mention-ts Latn">/šamaššammū/</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Xsux mention" lang="akk">𒊭𒈦𒌑𒈨</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ts mention-ts Latn">/šamaššammi/</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">oil plant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***setter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:setter.html>setter</a> (79660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">settere</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">set</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:setter.html>setter</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">zetter</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de"><a href = vnd.unilang:setter.html>Setter</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Setzer</i>. 
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:setter.html>setter</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:setters.html>setters</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who <a href = vnd.unilang:sets.html>sets</a> something, especially a typesetter.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The exam <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> so hard <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> assumed the question <b><a href = vnd.unilang:setter.html>setter</a></b> must have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> in a bad mood.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Some crossword <b><a href = vnd.unilang:setters.html>setters</a></b> work for various newspapers under different pseudonyms.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A long-haired breed of gundog (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Setter_(dog_breed)" class="extiw" title="w:Setter (dog breed)">Wikipedia</a>).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">She <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:spaniel.html>spaniel</a> and a red <b><a href = vnd.unilang:setter.html>setter</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1931</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Palmer_(author)" class="extiw" title="w:John Palmer (author)">Francis Beeding</a>,  “7/2”, in  <cite>The Norwich Victims</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL245514W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The two Gordon <b><a href = vnd.unilang:setters.html>setters</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> obediently to <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Oswald Feiling winced as he <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> to go home. He <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> felt a warning twinge of lumbago.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">volleyball</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The player who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> responsible for setting, or passing, the ball to teammates for an attack.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Object-oriented_programming" class="extiw" title="w:Object-oriented programming">object-oriented programming</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A function used to modify the value of some property of an object, contrasted with the getter.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in combinations</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A game or match that lasts a certain number of <a href = vnd.unilang:sets.html>sets</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> June 29,  Kevin Mitchell,  “Roger Federer back from Wimbledon 2012 brink to beat <a href = vnd.unilang:julien.html>Julien</a> Benneteau”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Guardian" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Guardian">The Guardian</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20161115072742/https://www.theguardian.com/sport/2012/jun/29/roger-federer-wimbledon-2012-julien-benneteau">[2]</a></sup>, archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/sport/2012/jun/29/roger-federer-wimbledon-2012-julien-benneteau">the original</a> on <span class="mw-formatted-date" title="2016-11-15">15 November 2016</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> desperately close until all but the closing moments, and for that <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> the 32nd-ranked <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Julien_Benneteau" class="extiw" title="w:Julien Benneteau">[<a href = vnd.unilang:julien.html>Julien</a>] Benneteau</a> to thank for bringing the fight out in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roger_Federer" class="extiw" title="w:Roger Federer">[<a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>Roger</a>] Federer</a>, whose thirst for these long battles <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> waned <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the past couple of years. For a player regarded by many as the greatest of all time his record in completed five-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:setters.html>setters</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ordinary: now 20 wins, 16 losses.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>One who hunts victims for sharpers.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Shakespeare to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>One who adapts <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> to music in composition.</li>
<li>A shallow seggar for porcelain.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of <a href = vnd.unilang:ure.html>Ure</a> to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***shamrock.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:shamrock.html>shamrock</a> (88239)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">seamróg</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">semróc</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">semar</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">semair</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*semarā</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*semaris</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">uisumaris</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*semh₁r-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*smeh₁r-</i>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">smári</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and possibly <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georgian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Georgian language">Georgian</a></span> <i class="Geor mention" lang="ka">სამყურა</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ka-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samq̇ura</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shamrock.html>shamrock</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">shamrocks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The trefoil leaf of any small clover, especially <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Trifolium_repens" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Trifolium repens"><i>Trifolium repens</i></a></span>, or such a leaf from a clover-like plant, commonly used as a symbol of Ireland.
<dl><dd><i>She wore a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shamrock.html>shamrock</a></b> in honor of her Irish ancestry.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any of several small plants, forms of clover, with trefoil leaves, especially <i>Trifolium repens</i>.
<dl><dd><i>The fields <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> covered with <b>shamrocks</b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">trefoil leaf</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">trefoil</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">any of several small plants</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">clover</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">trefoil</span></li></ul>
</body>

***shand.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:shand.html>shand</a> (53270)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">shande</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:schande.html>schande</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:schenden.html>schonde</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sċeand</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sċand</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shame, disgrace, infamy, ignominy, confusion; a shameful, infamous, or abominable thing; that which brings disgrace, scandal, disgraceful thing; a bad or infamous person, a buffoon, <a href = vnd.unilang:charlatan.html>charlatan</a>, wretch, imposter, recreant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skandō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shame, disgrace</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)ḱem-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cover, hide, conceal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schande.html>schande</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shame, disgrace, reproach, dishonour, scandal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:schande.html>Schande</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shame, disgrace, ignominity, dishonour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="Latn" lang="en">shame</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">shend</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shand.html>shand</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Shame; scandal; disgrace.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Base coin.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shand.html>shand</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:shand.html>shand</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:shand.html>shand</a></b>)

***shank.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a> (34691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">schanke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sċeanca</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">scanca</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skankô</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">skonk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Schanke</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schenkel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:skank.html>skank</a></i>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skankaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">skakkr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wry, crooked</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)keng-</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Irish">Middle Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mga">scingim</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I spring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σκάζω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skázō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to limp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shanks.html>shanks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The part of the <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> between the knee and the ankle.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1599</b>,  William Shakespeare,  <cite>As you like it</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">His youthful hose, well <a href = vnd.unilang:saved.html>saved</a>, a world too wide / For his shrunk <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a></b> […] (II.7)</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Meat from that part of an animal.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ornithology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A redshank or greenshank, various species of Old World wading <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> in the genus <i>Tringa</i> having distinctly colored <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a>.</li>
<li>A straight, narrow part of an object, such as a key or an anchor; shaft; <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a>.</li>
<li>The handle of a pair of <a href = vnd.unilang:shears.html>shears</a>, connecting the ride to the neck.</li>
<li>The center part of a fishhook between the eye and the hook, the 'hook' being the curved part that bends toward the point.</li>
<li>A protruding part of an object, by which it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> or can be attached.</li>
<li>The metal part on a curb bit that falls below the mouthpiece, which length controls the severity of the leverage action of the bit, and to which the reins of the bridle are attached.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A poorly played golf shot in which the ball <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> struck by the part of the club head that connects to the shaft.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1953</b>,  Arnold Gingrich,  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:esquire.html>Esquire</a> Treasury</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">To a good golfer a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> disgracefuller than being dead drunk or in jail.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An improvised stabbing weapon; a shiv.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>loop</a> forming an eye to a button.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The space between two <a href = vnd.unilang:channels.html>channels</a> of the Doric triglyph.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Gwilt to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metalworking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A large ladle for molten metal, fitted with long <a href = vnd.unilang:bars.html>bars</a> for handling it.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The body of a type; between the shoulder and the foot.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">shoemaking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The part of the sole beneath the instep connecting the broader front part with the <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a>.</li>
<li>Flat-nosed pliers, used by opticians for nipping off the edges of pieces of glass to make them round.</li>
<li>The end or remainder, particularly of a period of time.</li>
<li>The main part or beginning of a period of time.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a></b> of the morning</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1945</b>,  Tennessee Williams,  <cite>The Glass <a href = vnd.unilang:menagerie.html>Menagerie</a></cite>, page 92:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><small><a href = vnd.unilang:amanda.html>Amanda</a></small>: Going now? You're joking! Why, it's only the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a></b> of the evening, <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>’Connor!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shank.html>shank</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shanks.html>shanks</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shanking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shanked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ulster" class="extiw" title="w:Ulster">Ulster</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To travel on foot.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To stab, especially with an improvised blade.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To remove another's trousers, especially in jest; to depants.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> golf</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To misstrike the ball with the part of the club head that connects to the shaft.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly tennis<span class="ib-comma">,</span> soccer</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To hit or kick the ball in an unintended direction.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> September 28,  <a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>Tom</a> Rostance,  “Arsenal 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 1 Olympiakos”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/14998317.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Marouane Chamakh then spurned a great chance to kill the game off when he <a href = vnd.unilang:ran.html>ran</a> onto Andrey Arshavin's lofted through ball but <b>shanked</b> his shot horribly across the face of goal.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To fall off, as a leaf, flower, or capsule, on account of disease affecting the supporting footstalk; usually followed by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">off</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Darwin to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<dl><dd><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to stab with an improvised weapon</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> shiv <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></dd>
<dd><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to remove another's <a href = vnd.unilang:pants.html>pants</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> depants <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></dd></dl>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
